                }
            }
        }).data('kendoTreeView');

            kendoTreeView.collapse(kendoTreeView.element.find(".k-item"));
        }
    })(jQuery);

      <div class="searchdropbox">


    <input id="search" type="text" maxlength="100" />
    <input id="btnsearch" type="button" value="SEARCH" />
    <input id="searchsite" type="hidden" value='' />
    <input id="searchfields" type="hidden" value='' />

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#btnsearch").click(function () {
            GSA_ExecuteSearch();
            return false;
        });
        $("#search").keypress(function (e) {
            if (e.which == 13) {
                GSA_ExecuteSearch();
            }
        });
    });

    function GSA_ExecuteSearch()
    {
        var searchquery = $('#search').val();
        //alert(searchquery);
        if (searchquery != '') {
            var searchlink = "/search-results/" + "?q=" + encodeURI(searchquery);
            if ($('#searchsite').val() != '') {
                searchlink += "&site=" + encodeURI($('#searchsite').val());
            }
            if ($('#searchfields').val() != '') {
                searchlink += "&getfields=" + encodeURI($('#searchfields').val());
            }
            //alert(searchlink);
            window.location = searchlink;
        }
    }
</script>
</div>

    <div class="sf_colsOut sf_1col_1_100">
        <div id="srh5Content_TB09997DD015_Col00" class="sf_colsIn sf_1col_1in_100" style="margin: 30px 0px;"><div class="sf_cols homeBlogs">
    <div class="sf_colsOut sf_2cols_1_33" style="width: 33%;">
        <div id="srh5Content_C017_Col00" class="sf_colsIn sf_2cols_1in_33" style="margin: 0px 12px 0px 16px;"><div class='sfContentBlock'><h1>The AADE Blog</h1>


</div><div class='sfContentBlock'><h3>Featured Post:</h3>


</div>

        <ul class="sfpostsList sfpostListTitleDateSummary sflist">
            
        <li class="sfpostListItem sflistitem" data-sf-provider='OpenAccessDataProvider'  data-sf-id='3b1be636-a05f-6873-9c53-ff0000b8561d' data-sf-type="Telerik.Sitefinity.Blogs.Model.BlogPost">
            
            <h2 class="sfpostTitle sftitle">
                <a data-sf-field="Title" data-sf-ftype="ShortText" href="news/aade-blog/aade-blog-details/aade/2018/03/15/understanding-population-health-where-does-the-diabetes-educator-fit">Understanding Population Health: Where Does the Diabetes Educator Fit?</a>
            </h2>
            
            <div class="sfpostAuthorAndDate sfmetainfo">
                
              <div class="sfrelatedItmWrp" style="padding-bottom: 20px;">
                    <img src='https://www.diabeteseducator.org/images/default-source/default-album/gettyimages-837604444_850x420.png?sfvrsn=0' alt='GettyImages-837604444_850x420' title='GettyImages-837604444_850x420' style='margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px; background: white; 
            border-radius:10px; 
            -moz-border-radius:10px; 
            -webkit-border-radius:10px; 
            width: 100%;
            max-width: 500px; 
            height: auto' />
                </div>
              
                Mar 15, 2018
            </div>

            <div class="sfpostSummary sfsummary" data-sf-field="Summary" data-sf-ftype="ShortText">
	What is population health? AADE President Donna Ryan describes just what population health is and the opportunity for diabetes educators to be leaders.
</div>
        
          <div class="buttonwrapc buttonc"><a id="ctl00_srh5Content_C012_masterBlogPostsFrontend_ctl00_ctl00_Repeater_ctrl0_FullStory" href="news/aade-blog/aade-blog-details/aade/2018/03/15/understanding-population-health-where-does-the-diabetes-educator-fit">Full story</a></div>

        </ul>

<script type="text/javascript">    
    function successXMLsrh5Content_C015_rssarticles(xml) {
        var rssmaxarticles = 2;
        var rssshowdate = true;
        var rssmaxchar = 200;
        var rssfeedtitle = '';
        var rssshowsummary = true;
        if (rssfeedtitle.length > 0){
            $('#srh5Content_C015_rssarticles').append('<h2 class="feed-title">' + rssfeedtitle + '</h2>');
        }
        if (rssmaxarticles <= 0){
            rssmaxarticles = $(xml).find('entry').length;
        }        
        $(xml).find('entry').slice(0, rssmaxarticles).each(function () {
            var thisDate = new Date($(this).find('updated').text());
            var thisArticle = '<div class="rssArticle"><a class="pub-title" href="' + $(this).find('link').attr('href') + '">' + $(this).find('title').text() + '</a>';
            if (rssshowdate) {
                thisArticle += '<span class="pub-date">' + String(thisDate.getMonth() + 1) + "/" + String(thisDate.getDate()) + "/" + String(thisDate.getFullYear()) + '</span>';
            }
            if (rssshowsummary){
                var thisDescription = $(this).find('summary').text();
                //alert(thisDescription);
                if (rssmaxchar > 0) {
                    while (thisDescription.indexOf("<") > -1) {
                        var removedtag = '';
                        if (thisDescription.indexOf("<") > 0) {
                            removedtag = thisDescription.substr(0, thisDescription.indexOf("<"));
                        }
                        removedtag += thisDescription.substr(thisDescription.indexOf(">") + 1);
                        thisDescription = removedtag;
                    }
                    //alert(thisDescription);
                    var rssshortened = false;
                    while (thisDescription.length > rssmaxchar) {
                        rssshortened = true;
                        var periodspace = thisDescription.lastIndexOf(".");
                        if (periodspace < thisDescription.lastIndexOf(" ")) {
                            periodspace = thisDescription.lastIndexOf(" ");
                        }
                        thisDescription = thisDescription.substr(0, periodspace);
                    }
                    //alert(thisDescription);
                    if (rssshortened && thisDescription.lastIndexOf(".") != thisDescription.length) {
                        thisDescription += '...';
                    }
                    //alert(thisDescription);
                }
                thisArticle += '<div>' + thisDescription + '</div></div>';
            }            
            $('#srh5Content_C015_rssarticles').append(thisArticle);
        });
    }
    function callrsssrh5Content_C015_rssarticles() {
        var rssurl = 'http://www.myaadenetwork.org/f/bl/3-2-5-4-1-6-8-7-10-11-12-13-117-15-14-16-17-18-21-20-19-22-23-25-24-26-29-33-30-31-32-34-27-28-35-36-37-38-40-41-42-43-44-45-47-46-48-50-49-51-175';
        var rssdata = '';
        var rssheader = '';            
        $.ajax({
            data: { "Url": rssurl, "Data": rssdata, "Header": rssheader  },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                $('#srh5Content_C015_rssarticles').html(thrownError);
            },
            success: successXMLsrh5Content_C015_rssarticles,
            type: 'POST',
            url: "/vtc.rss"
        });
    }
    $(document).ready(callrsssrh5Content_C015_rssarticles);    
</script>
